\setkeys{format}{height=27.5pt,width=45pt,fsize=3pt,fskip=4pt,stretch=0.2,cols=12}%

\newcommand{\cols}{\format@cols}%
\newcommand{\labelbox}[1]{\parbox[t]{\format@width}{#1}\newline}%
\renewcommand{\baselinestretch}{\format@stretch}%
\newcommand{\lgen}{\raggedright

\makeatother%
